<h1 class="display-4 text-dark mb-4">Testimonials from our learners</h1>
<div class="px-md-6 px-3 py-3" #F5F5F5;">
<div class="text-center learner_blockquote">
<i class="fas fa-quote-left"></i>
<div id="carouselExampleIndicators" class="carousel slide">
<ol class="carousel-indicators mt-6">
<li class="bg-secondary"></li>
<li class="bg-secondary"></li>
<li class="bg-secondary"></li>
<li class="bg-secondary"></li>
<li class="bg-secondary active"></li>
<div class="carousel-inner pb-6">
<div class="carousel-item">
I just want to let you know that IITM and its team is doing an amazing job running this
program. I'm really
lucky to be enrolled into this program. I have never ever received replies for any
emails
within one day
from other universities. I know how difficultit is to reply to a lot of emails. Not only
that, right from
the program design and course content, every minute things are well planned and carried
out.
Hats off to
your team. Thank you for your support and guidance.
<h5 class="text-dark font-weight-bold mb-0">S Nithish Kumar </h5>
<div class="font-italic text-dark">
from Coimbatore, Tamil Nadu, India
<div class="carousel-item">
I would like to thank the whole team of IITM Online Degree for coming up with the
concept of
solving
questions with the professors. It has not only helped me in improving my performance
drastically in graded
assignments, but also it plays a relevant role in making the concepts more clear. Though
because of my
college schedule I am not able to attend all the live sessions, its recorded form is
proving
to be very
effective for me. A special mention for Prof.Andrew Thangaraj - his tips on problem
solving
are really
helpful. Once again thank you very much for understanding the requirements of the
students.
<div class="learner_sign">
<h5 class="text-dark font-weight-bold mb-0">Parth Shukla </h5>
<div class="font-italic text-dark">
from Lucknow, Uttar Pradesh, India
<div class="carousel-item">
I want to thank the team of IIT Madras who are making this Degree happen for us. I am
one of those students who had to face many financial and health issues in the early part
of their lives. And studying in IIT is only a dream for students like us. However, this
degree program (while maintaining the standard of IIT) has given us a chance to grow and
improve in our lives.
Also, I have personally checked many online programs by many Institutes and Universities
- however, none of them is so inspiring, innovative and challenging (at the same time).
It's such a great initiative of IIT Madras. I can't thank you enough and all the people
who are involved in making it happen. I want to specially thanks Prof. Andrew and Prof.
Pratap for clarifying all our doubts and also the professors and course support team -
without which I could have never qualified this process.
<div class="learner_sign">
<h5 class="text-dark font-weight-bold mb-0">Yash Raj Karthikey</h5>
<div class="font-italic text-dark">
from Bengaluru, Karnataka, India
<div class="carousel-item">
My name is Akriti Vishwas, I come from Lakhimpur Kheri, Uttar Pradesh.
I came across this online degree program on the internet. I just completed my 12th
standard and was enrolled in a bachelor degree in Hansraj College of Delhi University
pursuing physics honours. Apart from my degree I wanted to explore something new. This
program from such an esteemed institution like IIT MADRAS seemed exciting to me. The
unique program captured my attention and I enrolled for the qualifier level. The ever
increasing career opportunities in data science also contributed in a positive way.
After taking the classes from such qualified faculty, my interest in the program grew.
The unique pedagogy used by the teachers is what I found most engaging. The dedicated
support team also helped many learners like me at all times if we faced any
difficulties. Now, after qualifying the first level and being a student of the
foundational level, I am looking forward to this course and learning in a unique and
first of its kind way.
<div class="learner_sign">
<h5 class="text-dark font-weight-bold mb-0">Akriti Vishwas</h5>
<div class="font-italic text-dark">
from Lakhimpur Kheri, Uttar Pradesh, India

though we haven't met, it
doesn't like that due to amazing interaction and course planning of Bsc course
of IIT Madras.
They are managing at such a level without disturbing the standard of IIT. Hats
off to the team at IIT
Madras.
Feeling proud to be a part of such a great program.

<p></p><p>Dear Students,<br><br>IIT Madras has mandated that all students of all programs should mandatorily complete the POSH – Becoming Gender Sensitive training course, as part of the institute’s commitment to maintaining a safe and respectful learning environment for everyone.<br><br><strong>Module Link : <a href="https://seek.onlinedegree.iitm.ac.in/courses/ns_posh?id=14" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow noreferrer">https://seek.onlinedegree.iitm.ac.in/courses/ns_posh?id=14<br></a></strong><br>Please access the course from your student mail id.<br>We request you to ensure that the course is completed on or before 29th March 2026. It comprises a 1hr video along with a test that should be taken and submitted.<br><br></p><p></p>

<p class="reporting" id="reporting" 0px;"> Reporting harassment: IITM BS Degree Team is committed to ensuring that everyone is equally valued and treats one another with respect. All complaints of bullying or harassment will be taken seriouly and will be dealt with quickly and with respect for all people involved. Learners may write to this email id students-grievance@study.iitm.ac.in which will be considered as a formal complaint. We will make reasonable and appropriate efforts to preserve an individual's privacy and protect the confidentiality of information.</p>

All complaints of bullying or harassment will be taken seriouly and will be dealt with quickly and with respect for all people involved. Learners may write to this email id students-grievance@study.iitm.ac.in which will be considered as a formal complaint. We will make reasonable and appropriate efforts to preserve an individual's privacy and protect the confidentiality of information.</p>

<section class="foundation_level mt-4 col-11">
<p class="reporting" id="reporting" 0px;"> Reporting harassment: IITM BS Degree Team is committed to ensuring that everyone is equally valued and treats one another with respect. All complaints of bullying or harassment will be taken seriouly and will be dealt with quickly and with respect for all people involved. Learners may write to this email id students-grievance@study.iitm.ac.in which will be considered as a formal complaint. We will make reasonable and appropriate efforts to preserve an individual's privacy and protect the confidentiality of information.</p>
<p id="contact_support" class="reporting">For any other queries or issues, <a href="https://study-supportdesk.freshdesk.com/support/login" target="_blank">click here</a> to report them or ask for support</p>

All complaints of bullying or harassment will be taken seriouly and will be dealt with quickly and with respect for all people involved. Learners may write to this email id students-grievance@study.iitm.ac.in which will be considered as a formal complaint. We will make reasonable and appropriate efforts to preserve an individual's privacy and protect the confidentiality of information.</p>

<h2 class="dashboard-heading">
Student Certificates
<div class="dashboard-content">
<div id="student_documents_table_wrapper" class="dataTables_wrapper no-footer"><div class="dataTables_length" id="student_documents_table_length"><label>Show <select name="student_documents_table_length" class=""><option value="10">10</option><option value="25">25</option><option value="50">50</option><option value="100">100</option></select> entries</label></div><div id="student_documents_table_filter" class="dataTables_filter"><label>Search:<input type="search" class="" placeholder=""></label></div><table id="student_documents_table" class="display dataTable no-footer" role="grid">
<tr role="row"><th class="sorting_asc" tabindex="0" rowspan="1" colspan="1" 519.805px;"
Certificate Type
: activate to sort column descending">
Certificate Type
</th><th class="sorting" tabindex="0" rowspan="1" colspan="1" 375.195px;"
Certificate
: activate to sort column ascending">

<p class="reporting" id="reporting" 0px;"> Reporting harassment: IITM BS Degree Team is committed to ensuring that everyone is equally valued and treats one another with respect. All complaints of bullying or harassment will be taken seriouly and will be dealt with quickly and with respect for all people involved. Learners may write to this email id students-grievance@study.iitm.ac.in which will be considered as a formal complaint. We will make reasonable and appropriate efforts to preserve an individual's privacy and protect the confidentiality of information.</p>
<p id="contact_support" class="reporting">For any other queries or issues, <a href="https://study-supportdesk.freshdesk.com/support/login" target="_blank">click here</a> to report them or ask for support</p>

<p class="reporting" id="reporting" 0px;"> Reporting harassment: IITM BS Degree Team is committed to ensuring that everyone is equally valued and treats one another with respect. All complaints of bullying or harassment will be taken seriouly and will be dealt with quickly and with respect for all people involved. Learners may write to this email id students-grievance@study.iitm.ac.in which will be considered as a formal complaint. We will make reasonable and appropriate efforts to preserve an individual's privacy and protect the confidentiality of information.</p>
<p id="contact_support" class="reporting">For any other queries or issues, <a href="https://study-supportdesk.freshdesk.com/support/login" target="_blank">click here</a> to report them or ask for support</p>

<h2 class="dashboard-heading mb-4">Pending Payments</h2>
<div class="dashboard-content">
<p class="text-dark">No pending payments.</p>
<p class="reporting" id="reporting" 0px;"> Reporting harassment: IITM BS Degree Team is committed to ensuring that everyone is equally valued and treats one another with respect. All complaints of bullying or harassment will be taken seriouly and will be dealt with quickly and with respect for all people involved. Learners may write to this email id students-grievance@study.iitm.ac.in which will be considered as a formal complaint. We will make reasonable and appropriate efforts to preserve an individual's privacy and protect the confidentiality of information.</p>

<h2 class="dashboard-sub-heading">Mandatory POSH Training for All Students</h2>
<p></p><p>Dear Students,<br><br>IIT Madras has mandated that all students of all programs should mandatorily complete the POSH – Becoming Gender Sensitive training course, as part of the institute’s commitment to maintaining a safe and respectful learning environment for everyone.<br><br><strong>Module Link : <a href="https://seek.onlinedegree.iitm.ac.in/courses/ns_posh?id=14" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow noreferrer">https://seek.onlinedegree.iitm.ac.in/courses/ns_posh?id=14<br></a></strong><br>Please access the course from your student mail id.<br>We request you to ensure that the course is completed on or before 29th March 2026. It comprises a 1hr video along with a test that should be taken and submitted.<br><br></p><p></p>

<h2 class="dashboard-sub-heading">Announcement For End term City Change (September Term)</h2>
<p></p><p>Dear student, <br>&nbsp;<br>The Option to edit the exam city preference for End term is available in your dashboard under exam cities and hall tickets. Based on multiple requests We have extended the deadline.<br>&nbsp;<br><span #ffff00;"><strong><span #000000;">Last date to edit the exam city is &nbsp;(11/11/22 at 5PM IST). </span></strong></span><br>&nbsp;<br>Students who are willing to change from India to outside India or from outside India to India have to mail to <a href="mailto:support@onlinedegree.iitm.ac.in" target="_blank">support@onlinedegree.iitm.ac.<wbr>in</a> to get a g-form. <br><strong>Deadline for G-form is (11/11/22 at 5PM IST).</strong><br>&nbsp;<br>We request students to select the exam city considering all your situation (college opens, college closes etc.,). No more changes will be entertained after the deadline<br>&nbsp;<br><strong>NOTE <span #ffffff; color: #ff0000;">: There will not be any change in Quiz2 exam city. This announcement is only for the end term exam.</span></strong></p><p></p>

## [About the Course :: IITM Online Degree](https://seek.onlinedegree.iitm.ac.in/courses/ns_26t1_cs1002?id=2)
